Suzhou 99

Water Conservancy Association Assists in Building a Long Dyke in the Lake: The east and west mountains in Taihu Lake in the county stand opposite each other, and transportation is impossible without boats. Therefore, lake bandits have occupied Mingwan and other places, harassing travelers. When the troops rush to suppress the bandits, they flee and it is impossible to catch them. During the county-wide administrative meeting last winter, Zhu Liang, the district chief of the 19th district in the West Mountain, proposed to build a long dike to connect the two mountains so that travelers would not be in danger and the police team could easily capture the bandits. The plan was passed and a plan was prepared, passing through the West Mountain, the Big and Small Turtle Mountains, and reaching the Lutang Town on the East Back Mountain, which is more than ten miles long. County Chief Huang sent a letter to the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Committee for verification. The Water Conservancy Committee replied that the construction of a long dike may hinder water conservancy and did not express approval. Subsequently, District Chief Zhu of the 19th District submitted a supplementary plan, considering both water conservancy and transportation. County Chief Huang sent a letter to the Water Conservancy Committee. The committee replied yesterday that the plan was still feasible and agreed to assist. After County Chief Huang approved the letter, he ordered the Construction Bureau to be responsible for actively designing it so that it could be built as soon as possible to benefit the people of the east and west mountains.

Mediation of Labor-Capital Disputes in the Incense Industry: Labor-capital disputes in the Wu County incense industry have been unresolved for several years. Since the capital side was ordered to reorganize the trade association last year, it has issued notices, but the labor side's trade union has not been able to integrate with the capital side. At the end of last month, the trade union requested the capital side to improve treatment and submitted a request to the county government for assistance, expressing laziness. County Chief Huang submitted the request to the Construction Department for verification. Yesterday (the 2nd), the Construction Department issued instructions to organize a mediation committee immediately. After receiving the order, County Chief Huang appointed Qian Tianpeng, the director of the Construction Bureau, Xu Woyun, a member of the county government, and Shi Junqing, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, as members of the mediation committee to carry out mediation.

Blood Case Caused by Love Affair Between Nun and Butcher: The Yuantong Nunnery near the Shanren Bridge in Mudu, a county town, adopted Yun Sheng, the three-year-old daughter of Chen Jinfu, a farmer in the village, as a young nun in 1915. She is now 19 years old and is quite beautiful. In the winter of the year before last, she was seduced by Xu Er, a sheep butcher from the same village, and Yun Sheng planned to grow her hair and make a lifelong agreement with Xu. Last year, Yun Sheng suddenly abandoned Xu Er and had an affair with the monks Xin Bao and Yun Kui of the nearby Sudun Temple. Xu Er found out about the affair and went to the Yuantong Nunnery with a sheep-slaughtering knife hidden in his home on the night before last. He went straight into the inner room and saw the two monks Xin Bao and Yun Kui inside, and a conflict broke out. The monks escaped. At that time, Xu Er was furious and stabbed Yun Sheng's legs twice before escaping. Afterwards, Yun Sheng's father reported the incident to the Mudu Public Security Fifth Branch Bureau. Director Zhang ordered the police to arrest Xu Er. Yesterday, he, Yun Sheng, Chen Jinfu, and others were sent to the city and transferred to the Public Security Bureau. Zhang asked Xu Er for questioning. According to Xu Er, he had been having an affair with Yun Sheng for as many as 150 times and pointed out the secret marks on Yun Sheng's private parts. After receiving the confession, Zhang transferred the case to the local court for verification.

President Lin Goes to Wujin for Inspection: President Lin of the High Court went to Wujin yesterday (the 2nd) morning with Yao Guozhang, the chief of the prison section, to inspect prison administration and visit the court because the Wujin County Court has been established since the establishment of the court, the litigation affairs are frequent, and the detention center and county prison hold a large number of prisoners. It is necessary to rectify the situation, and it is also necessary to dredge the flow of prisoners during this warm weather, which is prone to diseases.

Changshu 100

Wuxi 101

Actively Expanding Long-Distance Telephone Service in Nine Counties

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Electricity Management Office connected long-distance telephone service in nine counties in January of this year, business has been very slow, with monthly revenue of only about 60 yuan. The reason is the inconvenience of making calls, as the service only allows exchanges to communicate with each other. If the exchange is far away, the multiple transfers lead to many errors. Affected by this, the long-distance telephone service in the nine counties has not been able to develop. Recently, Deng Zaichen, the director of the Electricity Management Office, recognizing this, advocated connecting the telephone exchange in the exchange to the trunk lines of the Wuxi Telephone Company, so that callers can directly communicate with the destination, and the business scope can be expanded. He came to Wuxi the day before yesterday to discuss with Mao Feng, the director of the Construction Bureau, and the telephone company. The result was a decision to connect the poles and wires of the Wuxi four-township telephone east line to the Su-Chang line of the nine-county long-distance telephone service of the Electricity Management Office, and to connect the exchange telephone of the Su-Chang line to the telephone company. The Electricity Management Office also ordered a 30-line exchange from a Shanghai foreign firm. It has already been shipped from Shanghai to Wuxi, and the electrical materials have also been prepared, ready for immediate installation, and additional operators will be assigned to expand the business after connecting with the telephone company. Director Deng also sent Ruan Fengxiang, a staff member of the First Section, to Wuxi to investigate and negotiate the wiring issues with all parties. In order to universally install telephones in the four townships, the local Construction Bureau specially appointed Mr. Qian as the director of telephone engineering to be actively responsible for the project.

Bloody Tragedy at Lequan Bathhouse

The Lequan Bathhouse on Wanqian Road in this town has been very successful since its opening and has been quite profitable. Hui A’da paid 150 yuan to the manager, Xie Shaojing, to lease the special room in the bathhouse. Recently, Xie recommended his friend Xue Rongrui to work in the special room, in order to replace Hui A’da. After Rongrui entered the bathhouse, he relied on the power of Manager Xie and used various improper means to force Hui A’da to hand over all the items in the room one by one. Hui refused, and Xue harbored resentment. Yesterday (the 2nd) at 1:00 PM, Xue Rongrui went to the bathhouse to argue with Hui A’da. During the argument, they got into a fight. Xue Rongrui became angry and took a sharp knife and stabbed Hui A’da in the forehead three times in a row. Hui immediately fell to the ground unconscious in a pool of blood. The police at the scene sent the injured Hui A’da to the Rendeq Hospital on Jiaoji Road for treatment. At the same time, the assailant Xue Rongrui was arrested and sent to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau to be transferred to the General Bureau for delivery to the County Court to await legal questioning.

New Journalists’ Association Established

The local Journalists’ Association held its inaugural meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at the County Party Rectification Committee. Thirty-five members attended, including Sun Dexian, Hua Shixiang, Sun Boliang, Sun Chunpu, Feng Tiannong, and Shi Qinglin. Sun Dexian was elected chairman. Night Boat Robbed En Route

A night boat from Dangkou Town in Nanyan City travels between the city and the countryside every day. The day before yesterday at about 7:00 PM, the boat owner Yang Jinhai directed the boatman to set sail from the countryside to the city. While passing through Sushe Dang, they suddenly encountered a boat. Seven bandits jumped out of the boat with wooden sticks and iron bars, ordering them to stop the boat. They then jumped onto the boat one after another, threatening them into silence and looting at will for about two hours. They then jumped back to their original boat with their loot and sped away. The boat owner and passengers, seeing that the bandits had gone far away, checked their losses. Passengers had been robbed of more than 120 yuan, more than 80 yuan in entrusted goods, and clothing, for a total loss of more than 300 yuan. The boatmen then reported to the Seventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau, requesting that the police be sent to pursue the stolen goods. The Branch Chief immediately led the police to the scene, but the bandits had already disappeared without a trace.

Firefighting Conflict on Tonghui Road

More than 20 thatched sheds behind the first platform on Tonghui Road outside Guangfu Gate in this town suddenly caught fire the day before yesterday. When the fire was raging, members of the Eleventh Section of the Northern Road Security Fire Brigade rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm. However, when they arrived at the Gongyun Bridge, they were beaten indiscriminately by members of the Twelfth Section of the Northern Road Fire Brigade with weapons. As a result, Wang Abing, Wang A’da, Tang A’er, Shao Afu, and Liu Heshang were all bleeding from their heads and seriously injured in their chests and waists. At that time, the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau sent police to arrest the firefighters Tao Shungen and others involved in the incident and took them to the bureau. Yesterday, they were transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. The injured team members Wang Abing and others filed a complaint with the County Court requesting an examination of the injuries and requesting the immediate arrest of the fleeing suspects Gou Tou A’er, Xiao Doufu, Wang Fuquan, and Wang Fugen for investigation. At 4:00 PM, Prosecutor Zhu opened the court for questioning, examined the injuries, and ordered them to return home for treatment pending the trial of the captured suspects Tao Shungen and others in accordance with the law.

Changzhou 102

Strike at Wansheng Iron Factory

The Wuyi Wansheng and Housheng Iron Factories have a total of more than 100 workers. Yesterday (April 1st) happened to be the time when the factory implemented a 10-hour workday. Workers Liu Xingsheng of the Wansheng Factory and Worker Wang of the Housheng Factory came out to oppose it. The day before, they had secretly met with workers from both factories at the City God Temple, intending to incite a strike. The factory learned of this and, fearing that it would cause a storm, summoned all the workers to the factory to persuade them to work as usual when work began on the morning of the 1st. At the same time, they asked the Public Security Bureau to send a pistol team to the factory to maintain order. However, five workers, including Liu Xingsheng and apprentice Wang Kunsheng of the Wansheng Factory, were still inciting a strike in the factory and, in the meantime, contacted the Housheng Factory to take united action. The manager of the factory, Wan Guoping, seeing the tense situation, discussed the matter with Team Leader Xu of the pistol team and others and took the workers Liu Xingsheng, apprentice Wang Kunsheng, and others to the bureau for temporary custody. However, three other apprentices, including Ding Yongzhao, escaped over the wall and secretly conspired with more than 100 workers and apprentices from the Housheng Factory on how to deal with the situation, so it has not been completely resolved.

Pinghu 106

Abbot of Large Temple Harbors Bandits

Among the bandits in eastern Pinghu, there is a small leader named Shui Ade, who is one of the most fierce bandits. He and Mingshan, the abbot of the Quan Gong Ting Large Temple, are sworn brothers. Ade was severely suppressed by the army and sneaked into the temple to hide. Mingshan gave him a cassock to disguise himself as a monk and escape. The Quan Shui police learned of this and went to the temple on March 31 to arrest Ade, but he had already escaped, and Mingshan had also fled. Seven monks were arrested, and after interrogation, it was found that the monks were all law-abiding monks, and they were released on bail.

County Qingxiang Bureau Established

The county government received a telegram from the Qingxiang General Bureau yesterday, which stated that according to the Qingxiang Regulations, the director of the Qingxiang Bureau of each county should be concurrently held by the county magistrate, and the deputy director should be concurrently held by the county public security chief. The county magistrate should be appointed first, and the county bureau should be established on schedule. The county party headquarters should be invited to swear in and report. After receiving the telegram, County Magistrate Wu and others followed the regulations and established the Qingxiang Bureau on April 1, and the seal of the Qingxiang Bureau of Pinghu County was engraved and took office on the same day.

The boat notified Dinghai Quality Mansion after arriving in Yong yesterday morning to inform Hu’s family.

Important Education News

Elementary School Music Textbooks Sent to Ministry for Review 109

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments of all provinces and cities, stating: "According to the report from Zhang Daofan, the director of the Education Department of Zhejiang Province, stating that 'According to the report from the United Association of Elementary Schools Attached to Zhejiang Provincial Middle Schools, stating that "Music is an important subject for cultivating emotions and promoting national spirit. The music textbooks currently used in general elementary schools are all gentle songs, which have a significant impact on children's temperament and the future of the nation. The third standing committee meeting of the association decided to request the Ministry of Education to compile elementary school music textbooks for use in all elementary schools. It is requested that the matter be reviewed and implemented." According to this, the music textbooks currently popular in general elementary schools and in the market are mostly unsuitable for children's temperament, and the tunes are weak, which does indeed have an impact on the future of the nation. It is requested that the Ministry compile elementary school music textbooks for use in all elementary schools. It is requested that the matter be reviewed and instructed for compliance.' Therefore, the contents of elementary school music books issued by various publishers are mostly unsuitable. This Ministry has already ordered all bookstores to submit these books for review. Many bookstores have complied with the order, but some have not submitted them for review and have issued them without authorization. You should immediately order all bookstores to submit all elementary school music books that have not yet been submitted to the Ministry for review to avoid omissions. It is also found that many elementary schools in various places have compiled their own music textbooks, which may be used for selection. You should immediately order that these self-compiled textbooks be submitted to the local education administrative organs, which will then be submitted to the Ministry for compilation and reference." In addition to the reply and separate orders, the above order is hereby issued for compliance."

Ministry of Education Orders Provinces and Cities to Draft Internship Regulations for European and American Students 110

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments of all provinces and cities, stating: "Now, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has issued document No. 646, stating that 'The proposal of the National Industrial and Commercial Conference last year to select specialized personnel to go to factories in various countries for internship is intended to use the help of others to increase knowledge and skills and promote the development of our country's industry. In addition to the Ministry trying to contact foreign factories and selecting specialized graduates to go for internship, it is also hoped that the current students studying abroad or students selected to study abroad in the future will, after graduation, ask the ambassadors of the country to introduce them to famous factories in the country to study one or two or three years of subjects currently needed, such as mechanical, electrical, chemical, metallurgical, textile, etc., and then return to the country for use. Now that construction is in full swing and talent is needed, it would be of great benefit to the future to broadly value talent and devote efforts to industry. However, the matter falls under the scope of your Ministry's management, and you are requested to review and handle it to create talent and promote the revitalization of industry.' It is hereby noted that students studying science and engineering abroad should pay special attention to internships so that theory can be confirmed. The Ministry of Industry's proposal that students be introduced to famous factories in foreign countries for internships after graduation by the embassies in order to become familiar with technical methods is very appropriate. In addition to the reply and a request to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct the embassies to comply, the Ministry has also issued instructions to the Student Supervision Office in Japan. It is hereby ordered that the department consider the funding and number of students studying in Europe and America in the province and draft internship regulations for graduates studying in Europe and America to be submitted to the Ministry for review."

Ministry of Education Issues Order Restricting the Establishment of Ordinary Middle Schools 115

Adding Vocational Schools With High and Junior-Level Agriculture and Industry Courses

Ordinary Middle Schools Should Add Vocational Courses or Vocational Subjects

County Middle Schools Should Be Affiliated or Converted to Rural Teachers' Schools and Vocational Courses

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments of all provinces and cities restricting the establishment of ordinary middle schools and increasing the number of vocational schools. The order calls for adding vocational courses or vocational subjects in ordinary middle schools and for county junior high schools to be affiliated with or converted to rural normal schools and vocational courses.

It is noted that China has been running schools for thirty years, but social production is backward, and people's livelihoods are increasingly difficult. The reason is that ordinary schools have never paid attention to vocational education. For example, the former Class A and B vocational schools and today's vocational schools are often limited to economic talents, relying only on book teaching and rarely engaging in practical work. Therefore, after graduation, students still lack the practical skills to engage in various production activities. Although there are also subjects such as handicrafts, agriculture, and industry in the curricula of ordinary primary and secondary schools, in reality, they are mostly superficial and empty, and the teaching efficiency is naturally poor. This is a common problem of primary and secondary schools, both past and present, but its harm is particularly evident in today's middle schools. Originally, middle school education was preparation for further education and employment. Given the current economic difficulties of the Chinese people, middle-class families find it difficult to provide their children with a university education. Therefore, most middle school graduates cannot continue their studies. Because there are few vocational schools or their performance is not yet remarkable, most primary school graduates flock to ordinary middle schools. School organizers do not observe and mistakenly believe that education has developed in recent years and that many primary school graduates are promoted to higher education. Therefore, they think that it is not enough to increase the number of middle schools. As a result, provinces and cities compete to run high schools, and counties and cities compete to run junior high schools. Even districts below the county level have established middle schools, and private school organizers seem to have no schools to run other than middle schools. The proliferation of public and private middle schools in various places today and the low standards are all due to this one-sided observation. Therefore, after students graduate, they have no vocational training and cannot engage in various occupations. They also overestimate themselves and cannot choose a job like primary school graduates. They are at a loss and do not know what to do. Ordinary middle schools are therefore criticized by the world. If this situation does not change, we will see the exhaustion of people's livelihoods and the stagnation of society, with no end in sight. Foreseeing the future fills us with worry. Since unification, the central government has deeply considered the plan for a century and promulgated the educational purpose of the Republic of China, which is "to enrich the people's lives, support social survival, develop the people's livelihood, and continue the life of the nation based on the Three People's Principles..." It is further stipulated in the implementation guidelines that ordinary education must "cultivate the people's living skills and increase the people's productive capacity..." Reviving the decline and saving the ills are almost impossible. In order to correct the current malpractice and implement the educational purpose and its implementation guidelines, the following guidelines are specifically formulated for the establishment of middle school education in each province and city:

1. Starting from the 20th year, provinces and cities directly under the Executive Yuan that have too many ordinary middle schools and too few vocational schools should temporarily not add ordinary high school courses and junior high schools. If the enrollment situation of ordinary high school courses in each province and city in the last two or three years shows that the number of applicants exceeds the number of those admitted by several times, the number of classes in each ordinary high school course may be appropriately increased.

2. Starting from the 20th year, provinces should add vocational schools with high and junior-level agriculture and industry courses according to the circumstances.

3. Starting from the 20th year, county middle schools should be gradually reorganized into vocational schools or rural normal schools. The method is to stop recruiting ordinary middle school students and recruit vocational or normal school students starting from the 20th year. Subsequent recruitment will be gradually changed. When all the original ordinary middle school students have graduated, they will be pure vocational schools or rural normal schools. If the counties really need to establish ordinary middle schools, those that are not reorganized should be ordered by the Education Department to attach vocational courses and rural normal school courses to the ordinary middle schools.

4. Starting from the 20th year, ordinary middle schools should uniformly add vocational subjects or attach vocational courses.

5. Vocational schools or middle schools with attached vocational courses should raise funds to enrich equipment and earnestly cultivate students' labor habits and production skills. The existing vocational schools at all levels should be increased with funding to expand them.

6. Starting from the 20th year, the counties and cities and private applicants who apply to establish ordinary middle schools should be supervised or persuaded to change to vocational schools such as agriculture and industry. However, if the location of the county and city is too far from the provincial middle school and it is verified that it is necessary, the establishment may be approved.

The education departments of each province and city (directly under the central government) should comply with the above guidelines and formulate implementation measures with reference to local conditions and report them to the Ministry before the end of the 19th year for review. This is very important.

Jiangsu Province Middle School Joint Sports Meet Ball Game Schedule 116

｜Participants｜ 20 Boys' Schools｜ 14 Girls' Schools｜

The Jiangsu Province Fourth Annual Middle School Joint Sports Meet is scheduled to be held from May 1st to 4th at the Zhenjiang Public Sports Field. This newspaper has learned that ball game registrations from all schools have been completed. There are 20 boys' schools and 14 girls' schools participating, totaling 19 boys' basketball teams, 10 tennis teams, 8 soccer teams, 10 volleyball teams, 4 girls' tennis teams, 6 volleyball teams, and 12 basketball teams. Due to the short duration of the meet and limited venues, the organizing committee deems it necessary to hold preliminary rounds in accordance with the regulations. We now present the full schedule and preliminary ball game rules below:

Preliminary Ball Game Rules 117

(1) All schools participating in the preliminary rounds must attend the competition at the location specified in the notice from the organizing committee. (2) The date and time of the competition shall be determined by the home team in consultation with the visiting team, but must not be later than April 15th. Absence will be considered a forfeit. (3) The referees for the competition shall be appointed by the home team in consultation with the visiting team. (4) The competition rules shall be those established by the National Games and the Chinese National Sports Federation. (5) After the competition, both sides shall record the names, positions, and scores of all participating players in detail on the competition report form, have it signed by the referee, and mail it to the organizing committee within three days after the competition. At the same time, the results should be sent to major newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai for publication. Failure to report will be considered a forfeit and will disqualify the team from participating in the following week's competition. (6) If any unfortunate problems arise during the competition, the details, along with the referee's official report, should be sent to the organizing committee by express mail on the same day for review and decision.

The King of Siam Arrives in Shanghai This Afternoon 123

Government Representatives Board the Ship to Welcome Him

The King of Siam, traveling on the Japanese Empress Liner from Hong Kong, is expected to arrive in Shanghai and dock at the Gong He Xiang Wharf in Pudong at 1:30 PM today. The National Government has made all preparations to welcome the King of Siam. Wang Zhengting, the Minister of Foreign Affairs representing the National Government, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing last night around 9:00 PM. He is scheduled to accompany aides Hu Shize, Liu Yunfang, and Bi Hongyu, along with Shanghai Mayor Zhang Qun, aides Yu Hongjun, representatives of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai, and representatives of the Ministry of Industries Zhao Jinqing, on the Jin Hui small steamship to Gong He Xiang Wharf in Pudong to welcome the King. The silk and tea gifts presented to the King of Siam by Chiang Kai-shek and his wife and Minister Wang will be transported to the Japanese Empress Liner by another small steamship. Preparations for security in Pudong and Puxi have also been completed.

Sa Fuchou and Others Have Been Escorted to Beijing 124

Sa Fuchou, the former commander of the Fuzhou Fortress in the Fujian Provincial Coup Case, Lin Zhong, the Brigade Commander of the Marine Corps and Commander of the Fuzhou Provincial Defense, and Qiu Zhenwu, the Deputy Brigade Commander, were arrested after arriving in Shanghai from Fujian. The commanders of various naval vessels had previously telegraphed Navy Minister Yang Shuzhuang, requesting that they be returned to the Navy Headquarters for handling in accordance with military law. It is now learned that this time, Sa and others came to Shanghai on the Changsha ship. The Municipal Government's actions were based on the central government's wanted order. They have now received orders and yesterday dispatched personnel to escort them to Beijing for investigation.

The commanders of the naval vessels stationed in Nanjing, Shanghai, and the Yangtze River telegraphed Yang Shuzhuang again yesterday, requesting the release of Sa, Lin, and Qiu. The Fujian Provincial Government, Minister Yang of the Navy, I address you secretly. My esteemed colleague Chen telegraphed inviting you to investigate. Now Sa Fuchou, Lin Zhong, and Qiu Zhenwu have been escorted to Beijing in the east. I have heard that your Excellency stated that these three are not without suspicion in the case of the January 6th coup. The Central Government has already punished Sa Fuchou and others with a major demerit and a three-month salary deduction. Your Ministry subsequently dismissed them from their posts. Later, the Central Government issued an amnesty order for those accused of political crimes. In this case, Sa Fuchou and others have been arrested again. This not only conflicts with the previous Central Government punishment and the Ministry's dismissal, but it also contradicts the Central Government's intention of leniency. I am deeply afraid and dare to implore your Excellency to quickly telegraph the Central Government to explain the details and request that Sa Fuchou and the other three be released.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Implements the Grand Yangtze River Shipping Plan 126

Since Li Zhonggong took over the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, he has felt the need for an active plan in terms of river and sea operations. Although it has been hindered by military transportation, preparations for expansion have continued unabated. He has been working hard to develop the Yangtze River route. Recently, the ships rented by the central government have been returned, and the riverboats can resume their routes on the Yangtze River one after another. The lack of ships upstream has made it impossible to connect the network. In terms of business, it is not only impossible to achieve the effect of unified command, but it is also regrettable to watch the good shipping business being taken by foreign ships. Now he has decided to implement his grand Yangtze River plan and promote its realization, and various facilities such as expanding shipping routes and adding ships are recorded below:

Increasing the Number of Ships to Xulu: In recent years, British, Japanese, and American shipping companies have been fiercely competing for river shipping in Sichuan. In addition to the Chongqing liners, they have also added the Yibin line upstream of the Sichuan River, which goes directly to Luzhou and Xufu ports. This route has the most freight, but the river is shallow and large ships cannot travel. Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nissin, and Jiejiang all have special shallow-water ships on this line. Now, in order to connect Southwest transportation and compete with foreign ships, China Merchants has decided to open this new Yibin shipping route, temporarily using two ships. The Shanghai office has purchased two shallow-water riverboats in the local area specifically for the new Xulu route. It is said that the purchase has been finalized, and as soon as the new ships are received, they will be sent to start service.

Adding Ships to the Hanyi Route: The company only has one fast ship, the Kuai Li, running on the Hanyi route, which gives the impression that there is too much cargo and too few ships. This year, Sanbei also added two ships. President Li, responding to the cargo and passenger demands of this route, has already agreed to send the Wenzhou liner Guangji from mid-month to Hankou specifically for the Yichang route. The Jiaohe ship will replace the Shanghai-Wenzhou line, and the Guangli ship, which runs the Nanhua line, will take over Jiaohe's Fuzhou route.

Expanding the Xiang River Line: There are no longer any bandits in Hunan, and industries such as rice, cotton, mineral sands, and tung oil are being shipped out in large quantities. Foreign ships are adding more ships, and since Li Yunliang rented the Liyuan ship on the Xiangtan-Changsha route last year, there have been two ships operating on this route. Now it still feels insufficient. It is planned to add another ship. Now Li Yunliang is renting a ship in Hankou to expand. In addition, the Changde route in Western Hunan has been suspended for a long time due to bandits. Now that the bandits have been suppressed, it can be opened. The company has also agreed to open a new shipping route in Western Hunan and has ordered the business department to prepare a plan.

Starting a Direct Shipping Route: Now, all the ocean merchants' ships of Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nissin, and Jiejiang have direct ships from Shanghai to Yichang. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company proposed opening the Shanghai-Yichang direct route last year, but it could not be realized due to the lack of ships for military transportation. Now that all the ships have been released, the company is considering running the Jiangda and Jiangjing ships on the Shanghai-Hankou to Yichang direct route. It will be implemented soon. Another Yangtze River direct route is planned for the North and South Ocean ships, which is from Shanghai to Hankou and then back to Shanghai before directly opening the routes to Yantai, Tianjin, Shantou, and Xiamen. This special route is not currently operated by any company. Once it is opened, it can avoid the trouble of transshipment. The company initially planned to run the Xinfeng and Gongping ships on this river-sea direct route. Later, due to the shortage of ocean ships, it was not enough to distribute. It will be possible to open the route after the ocean ships that have been purchased arrive.

Purchasing Ten Ocean Ships: President Li, in order to replenish the Xinkang, Xinji, Xinhua, and Xinchang ships that were lost and to expand the coastal routes, decided to purchase ten ocean ships. It is said that he plans to purchase part of them and build part of them. Therefore, he has already sent a letter to the Jiangnan Factory asking them to send the cheapest shipbuilding price and drawings of various classes of ocean ships so that they can contact and order the construction.

Shipping News 127

French Giant Ship Arrives in Shanghai: The largest new mail ship, the Rosso, built by the French Postal Ship Company, has a deadweight of 24,000 tons. The layout of various classes of passenger seats is excellent. It is the first giant ship in the Sino-French navigation administration. It arrived in China for its first maiden voyage yesterday. Its ticket price is higher than other ships. It is now scheduled to return to France on the 25th.

Negotiations on Cargo Ship Collision: The pottery cargo ship of the Zhensufactory, carrying 32,000 pieces of cargo, was sunk in front of the Taikoo Beijing Wharf in the Huangpu River. Shi Guicai was commissioned to salvage the ship. When it was being towed up, it was hit by Xin Jiangtian, the tow rope was broken, and it sank again. The salvage ship was also damaged, with a total loss of 2,300 yuan. He contacted the shipping department of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday, and they were thoroughly investigating the driving and collision of Xin Jiangtian at that time.

New Price for Piece Goods and Water Freight: The water freight for goods on the Yangtze River Shanghai-Hankou route increased by 30% starting from March 1st. It has been implemented for a long time. It is now heard that the customs brokers sent a letter to the shipping companies for piece goods, requesting the abolition of the measuring procedure. The Jardine Matheson Company sent a letter to Taikoo, Sanbei, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Ning Shao, Nissin, and other companies yesterday, requesting each to send representatives to Jardine Matheson to discuss the abolition of measuring. However, piece goods must be divided into cotton fabrics and woolen fabrics to set new prices separately. The water freight for flour has been slightly reduced. The new price list is as follows:

Shipped from Shanghai to:　Cotton Fabric per Piece　Woolen Fabric per Piece　Flour per Dan

Zhenjiang　Two Coins and Ten Cents　Two Coins and Twenty Cents　Two Coins and Twenty Cents

Nanjing　Two Coins and Twenty-Five Cents　Three Coins and Five Cents　Zero Coins and Twenty-Four Cents

Wuhu　Two Coins and Sixty-Five Cents　Three Coins and Sixty Cents　Zero Coins and Twenty-Six Cents

Jiujiang　Three Coins and Twenty-Five Cents　Four Coins and Forty-Five Cents　Zero Coins and Twenty-Seven Cents

The Sino-Dutch Foreign Affairs Support Association Pleads for Negotiations on the Dutch Tax Increase Case for the Third Time 128

The Sino-Dutch Foreign Affairs Support Association of the Republic of China, believing that the Dutch are despising the Chinese people and there are rumors that they have implemented an increase in entry tax, once again appealed to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to continue negotiations. The text of the telegram is recorded below: Minister of Foreign Affairs, Nanjing. In the previous telegram from Malaysia, the ministry continued to protest the Dutch tax increase case, but the Dutch claimed that it was a common law for treating expatriates from various countries and have not yet expressed acceptance. After reading it, I can see that the Dutch are completely unreasonable to me. First, the employment value of my country's expatriates is only one-tenth of that of Europeans and Americans, but the entry tax is levied equally, which is nominally equal but actually unequal. Second, my country's expatriates are the most numerous, exceeding those of other countries by hundreds of times. The increase in entry tax will harm my overseas Chinese the most, which is nominally equal but actually unequal. Third, the Dutch claim that this entry tax is a common law for treating expatriates from various countries. Why do they specifically designate the Chinese and indigenous people as a class in their regulations, which cannot be equal to Europeans, Americans, and Japanese? Their so-called laws are elastic like rubber, not firm and consistent like steel. When there are obligations, they are responsible for the Chinese to increase the burden. When there are rights, they specifically exclude the Chinese. This is not only the shame of the overseas Chinese but also the shame of the party and the country. Anyone with blood and courage will not be indignant. The association is based on supporting diplomacy and has the responsibility to contribute humble opinions. Together, we urgently telegram to plead with the ministry to continue to protest. On the one hand, we will inform the Dutch ambassador to China, and on the other hand, we will telegram the ambassador to the Netherlands to seriously negotiate. If they brazenly increase it, my country should immediately collect the same entry tax from the Dutch. The association should also unite with all sectors to boycott Dutch ships and Dutch products as a support for diplomacy and to avenge the shame of the people. I hope the ministry will educate them. The Sino-Dutch Foreign Affairs Support Association bows in winter.

News of the Silk Factory Strike in North Shanghai Yesterday 129

Complete Resumption of Work is Expected Today

More than 16,000 male and female workers from more than 20 silk factories in North Shanghai, such as Fengtai and Qingfeng, went on strike unanimously the afternoon before yesterday because their request to restore the original wages was not fulfilled. After the persuasion of the trade union and the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau, 22 silk factories, including Fuchangrun, resumed work yesterday. Workers from six silk factories, including Fumin, are still insisting on the strike. Two female workers were arrested yesterday. The details are recorded separately on the left.

Situation Yesterday Morning: At 4 AM yesterday morning, the various silk factories where the labor unrest occurred as usual urged the workers to go to work. The entire board of directors and staff of the North District Silk Spinning Industry Trade Union, Yuan Yunlong, Zhou Buyun, Li Tonghai, Wu Suzhen, Chen Qiaozhen, and others, more than ten people, set off before 4 AM to persuade the workers in the area of Chang'an Road, Guangfu Road, and Meiyuan Road to resume work first to avoid accidents. The restoration of the original wages is waiting for a legal solution. Therefore, around 6 AM, workers from 22 silk factories, including Fuchangrun, Yong'an, Xie'an, Baisi I, Baisi II, Baokang, Xie Feng, Longji, Qichang, Tailai, Dingkang, Shunfengyong, Xiechang, Xiexing, Yongtaixing, Yongyuan, Chunmei, Yuanyuan, Fengtai, Qingfeng Jin Yuan, and Shengyuan, resumed work one after another. The workers from six silk factories, including Fuchangtai at No. 695 Chang'an Road, Dingchangshun at No. 246 Hengfeng Road, Hengchangxin, Fumin at No. 238 Hengfengfeng Road, Baolun at No. 46 Yutong Road, and Dingyuan, are still insisting on the strike.

Female Workers Arrested: The Public Security Bureau of the Fourth District of Zhabei received information the day before yesterday

Afternoon, after learning about the silk factory workers' strike, they immediately dispatched more police officers near the silk factories to maintain law and order. At around 4 AM yesterday morning, two female workers who were suspected of inciting workers were suddenly seen at the corner of Chang'an Road and Meiyuan Road. They were arrested by the police officers of the Second Precinct of the Fourth District and taken to the district for questioning. They were then transferred to the Fourth District Headquarters for transfer to the Public Security Bureau for verification. According to the investigation, one of the arrested female workers, Wang Zhang, is 28 years old, from Yancheng, and is a female worker at the Fuchangtai Silk Factory. The other, Weng Lu, is 28 years old, from Taizhou, and is a female worker at the Jinyuan Silk Factory.

Dispatch Personnel for Investigation: The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau specifically dispatched Zhu Guilin, an employee of the Third Section, to the office of the North District Silk Spinning Industry Trade Union at No. 22 Quanlefang, Hengtong Road, and to the silk factories on Hengfeng Road, Chang'an Road, Guangfu Road, Meiyuan Road, and other places at 1 PM yesterday to conduct an on-the-spot investigation of the strike in order to report to the director and conduct mediation. Chen Xizeng, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, also dispatched personnel to Zhabei yesterday morning to investigate the detailed situation and advised the workers to resume work first and not to make mistakes. It is heard that as a result of the investigation and persuasion by the Social Affairs Bureau and the Public Security Bureau, a complete resumption of work is likely today.

The Real Estate Association Protests the Municipal Council's Valuation and Collection of Donations 130

The Shanghai Real Estate Association sent a letter to the Director-General of the Public Concession Municipal Council yesterday, saying, "It has been reported that your Council's collection of municipal general donations is based on estimated house rents, which destroys the long-standing conventions and municipal financial principles. Our Association believes that this is inappropriate. The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and the Shanghai Special District Citizens' United Association Preparatory Committee have all sent letters to your Council to criticize this. Now we ask your Council to immediately cancel this method. It should be known that the massive turmoil caused by the additional donations in 1927 was almost unmanageable. Fortunately, Mr. Yu Qiaqing mediated and resolved it peacefully. This method of collecting municipal general donations based on estimated house rents, calculated at a donation rate, is almost 1.4% higher than 1.2%. Avoiding the name of additional donations and making a huge additional donation is considered to be likely to cause major disputes, and the severity may be even greater than the 1927 additional donation.

In addition, your Council's land donations this year have been arbitrarily estimated higher, even by one and a half times. The annual income has increased a lot. However, the price of land is only expressed once during the transaction. It is not seen at ordinary times. It is reasonable to estimate the donation. A sudden increase will affect the burden of the owners and tenants, which is already very large. Our Association has previously expressed its opinion that it needs to be revised. Now your Council wants to increase the estimated rent higher than the actual rent in addition to the house rent with rental receipts, so as to increase the income. Or it is believed that it is quite beneficial to the landlords and can be used as an excuse to increase the rent. However, the landlords' costs have increased recently due to the increase in land donations, and the rental income is not as high as those who buy public bonds and deposit in banks. However, the tenants have been deterred. Therefore, many new buildings are empty. The income of municipal general donations has actually been affected. If your Council recalculates the municipal general donation based on the estimated rent higher than the actual rent, it will inevitably further reduce the tenants' rental ability, directly reduce the rental of real estate, and indirectly reduce your Council's tax loss. Killing the goose or chicken to get the golden eggs is a good analogy. Not only that, but the estimated rent of the rented house is higher than the actual one, then the estimated number of houses used for self-employment, such as residences and companies, which have no rent, will definitely increase accordingly. Those who are affected, such as major banks, major factories, and major department stores, will directly suffer the difficulties of increased burden, and indirectly will affect the industry and commerce. By then, all industries will decline, and transactions will be sharply reduced. Even if your Council wants to plunder and gather taxes, I am afraid that there will be no way to measure it. It is related to the social economy and the municipal prosperity and decline. We should do our best to give advice. We hope that we will still follow the old rules. In addition to the appropriate estimated rent for self-produced and self-used items, all municipal general donations will be calculated based on the actual rent. In addition, the Shanghai News reported a review on March 31, which I hope you will also review and pay attention to.

The Guangzhou-Wuzhou Air Mail Route is Opened 133

According to Shanghai Postal Authority news, an airmail route has been opened between Guangzhou and Wuzhou. The one-way flight time is one hour and forty minutes. All kinds of mail, such as letters, postcards, printed matter, and newspapers, can be sent through this route. However, in addition to the usual postage, airmail postage of 15 cents per 20 centimeters or fraction thereof must be paid according to weight. Parcels can also be sent through this route in the same way, but only those sent within Guangdong or Guangxi Province are allowed. All kinds of mail that need to be sent through this route and other airmail routes must also be subject to additional airmail postage.

County Government Proclamation on Diligent Compliance with Personal Registration 137

The Shanghai County Government issued a proclamation yesterday stating that the county's personal registration has been underway for several months, but many procedures are incomplete and omissions are numerous. This is partly due to ineffective handling and also due to the people's negligence. Now, under orders to carry out rural cleansing and census taking, if personal registration is not handled diligently, the effectiveness of the census will be lost in an instant, and household registration statistics will not be accurate, greatly affecting all matters related to local autonomy. Eight provisional measures are proposed, ordering each district chief to instruct township heads and neighborhood chiefs, and ordering the Public Security Bureau to instruct each sub-bureau to instruct police chiefs to comply diligently. The measures are also attached for public knowledge. Births, deaths, marriages, inheritances, separations, relocations, and disappearances must be reported to the district township offices for registration in a timely manner without delay, lest penalties be incurred. This proclamation is hereby issued.

Banking Law Does Not Apply to Qian Industry 138

Sugar Industry Association States Reasons

The Shanghai Sugar Industry Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "We respectfully inform you that we recently read in the newspaper that the Banking Law passed by the Legislative Yuan seems to include money shops (錢莊) within its scope. After translating the articles, we felt a great deal of concern. The money shop industry in our country has a long history. Such establishments exist in major cities and towns, as well as remote villages. Their business is mainly lending credit, and their organization is of unlimited liability, with shareholders bearing significant responsibility. China's industry and commerce are backward, capital is weak, and businesses of all sizes rely on credit loans for operating funds. Therefore, money shops rely on investing in various industries, and various industries depend on money shop loans for their survival. The two complement each other like lips and teeth, and their close relationship is self-evident. If the Banking Law were applied to money shops, their unlimited liability organization would change to limited liability, eliminating a good custom that has been followed for thousands of years. Those who have trusted and believed in them will become panicked. Furthermore, requiring shareholders to submit proof of property to the government will make potential entrepreneurs hesitant and make them give up. The money shop industry, which has been responsible for financing various industries, will inevitably be diminished, and those who have adjusted surpluses and deficits will also be hindered. Industries will lose their turnover, with no chance for development. The demise of industry and commerce can be expected imminently. Our association, as one of the various industries, feels it is our duty to speak out in the face of danger. Your esteemed Chamber leads all merchants, and we all share the same goal. We beg you to present the situation to the National Government, appealing for the formulation of separate money shop regulations based on the established customs of the money shop industry, so as to stabilize the money shop industry and indirectly maintain various industries. This urgent plea is submitted in the hope of your consideration and approval."

Moreover, this year is the time for the election of directors of the International Labor Bureau, which makes it even more difficult to ignore. Central Bank Inspection Report 145

85th Time

The 85th Central Bank Issuance Preparation Inspection Report stated: "In accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible notes by this bank. The 85th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on March 31, 1931. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: The total amount of convertible notes issued is 30,160,432 silver dollars, including 29,316,492 silver dollar notes and 843,940 silver dollar subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of reserve funds for convertible notes is 30,160,432 silver dollars, including 23,069,340.02 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 15,654,807.45 silver dollars deposited in the Issuance Bureau of this bank, 2,199,234 silver dollars deposited in branch banks in various ports, and 5,215,298.75 silver dollars deposited in peer banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 7,091,091.80 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in line with the regulations. This report is hereby made. Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank, March 31, 1931: Fu Xun, Supervisor Wang Jingli, Yuan Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jifei."

Foil Industry Asks to Reduce Business Tax 148

The Foil Industry Association fast-mailed a telegram: "Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing, please acknowledge receipt. On the day of the 8th, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter saying that the Ministry of Finance had approved a reply to the telegram, saying that the points raised should be handled, and we will wait for instructions from the Zhejiang Finance Department for review and reply before further review, etc., and so on, to the association. We should prepare a letter in reply and hope for your review, etc., and so on. We have been waiting quietly until now, and the tax rate has not been reduced, and the micro-collection method has not been corrected. Previously, tin foil completed a special tax of 12.5% in Zhejiang, and then it could circulate throughout the country without being re-collected. Since the government implemented the abolition of likin on New Year's Day this year, so as to relieve the suffering of merchants and people, the Zhejiang Provincial Government hastily announced and implemented a draft business tax on foil of 15% of the self-determined value, without the approval of your department. It violates the department's established outline, and the tax rate exceeds the department's promulgated outline by 65 times. On February 1st, merchants were recruited to handle it and renamed it the Jiangzhe Foil Special Business Tax. Its collection method is still based on the tax per cargo and sets up bureaus by district, which is no different from the previous likin card. Recently, the Shaoxing Tax Bureau has arbitrarily added a tax of nine cents of silver per piece of Shuangjiu tin foil, and customs everywhere often do not allow taxed goods to travel, which hinders sales and greatly affects business. Foil merchants are extremely distressed. This has been submitted to the general meeting for resolution and has been telegraphed to the Ministry for your consideration. We ask that the department consider the difficulties of merchants and approve the strict order of the Zhejiang Finance Department to reduce the business tax rate on foil and must comply with the departmental regulations. If one item and one tax can be implemented, circulating throughout the country without being re-collected, foil merchants will be grateful. Chen Yongnian, Xu Songjia, and Lu Bingyou, Chairman of the Delegates' Assembly of the Shanghai Foil Industry Association, bow."

Huang Bai Went to Taiwan to Investigate Tobacco and Returned to Shanghai 151

Mr. Huang Jiahu and his wife, Bai Zhiying, returned to Shanghai yesterday from a trip to Taiwan. According to Mr. Huang, this trip was to inspect the tobacco ban situation in Taiwan. Unexpectedly, during the period of leaving Shanghai, they were falsely accused of Bai Zhiying selling morphine, which is very hateful. However, because the police in Taiwan often pay attention to outsiders, and many friends report that someone wants to harm Mr. Huang, they had to take a little secrecy when leaving Shanghai. Someone visited Mr. Huang before departure, and his family said that Mr. Huang had gone to Hong Kong. There was originally a female anti-drug comrade from the United States who was supposed to go together, so Mrs. Huang was invited to go with her. Later, the American could not make the appointment due to the ship schedule, so Mr. and Mrs. Huang went alone, taking the route of Xiamen. On March 10th, they boarded the Fengshan Maru ship and arrived in Keelung the next day. They stayed in Taiwan for about a week. On March 19th, they boarded the Zhishalu ship of the Zhaohua Company and left Taiwan for Xiamen. They originally planned to transfer to the Zhijianpeng ship of the same company to Shanghai on the same day. Unexpectedly, after arriving in Xiamen, they learned that someone had falsely reported to the central government that Mrs. Huang was selling morphine. At the same time, a local merchant in Xiamen colluded with a gang and boarded the ship with great momentum, intending to kidnap Mr. Huang and secretly harm him by extraordinary means, making it impossible for Mr. Huang to declare his innocence. Fortunately, Mr. Huang negotiated with the captain of the Zhishalu ship and a certain gentleman from the company's Xiamen agent, who assisted righteously and sent an electric ship to escort him to a friend's place in the Gulangyu Public Concession for temporary shelter. The leaders of the local Public Works Department, who knew Mr. Huang's character, protected him. Mr. and Mrs. Huang stayed in that place for several months and originally planned to leave after receiving a telegram from Shanghai. They waited until the Taigu Company's Taiyuan ship sailed on the 29th and attached a ride to Shanghai. Before leaving, they were escorted to the ship by many anti-drug comrades in Xiamen, and strict precautions were taken before they could escape danger and arrive safely in Shanghai yesterday. This time, Mr. Huang received assistance from all parties in Xiamen and obtained evidence that a local merchant named Zhang colluded with certain people to falsely accuse Bai Zhiying. He plans to publish it one after another.

Local News II

The Three-Year-Old Murder Case Was Adjudicated Yesterday 152

Zhu Zhenqing Was Beaten to Death

Shen Yuezao Sentenced to One and a Half Years in Prison

The Defendant Still Applies for Appeal

In July of the 17th year of the Republic of China, Shen Yuezao, a patrolman No. 1244 of the Huizi Patrol Room, was searching pedestrians at the intersection of Elgin Road North and Zhejiang Road when Zhu Zhenqing, a tax collector from the Zhenjiang Municipal Finance Bureau, passed by. Shen insisted on checking him as usual, but Zhu, believing himself to be a civil servant, did not want to be searched by him, so a conflict ensued. They argued and then wrestled. Zhu suddenly fell to the ground, his face pale and appearing to be in a coma. He was sent to the hospital but died before treatment could be given. At that time, Zhu's wife, believing that her husband was beaten to death by Shen, hired a lawyer to sue the former Provisional Court, asking that he be punished according to the law. She also claimed that her husband had served in the Finance Bureau with a considerable monthly salary, and his family relied on it for support. Now that he had died in a non-fatal accident, she attached a private suit demanding that Shen compensate for the loss of more than 20,000 yuan in order to support his wife and children in the future. After several sessions of the former Provisional Court's trial, no judgment was made. The jurisdiction of the Concession was taken back by our country and the Special District Local Court was reorganized. Although this case was also included in the handover, it was delayed and no one had the time to deal with it. For three years, no one had paid attention to it. Recently, the Criminal Court President Zhou Han of the Special Court summoned both parties and inquired several times. Yesterday morning was the date for public debate on the case. The lawyers for both sides appeared in court and debated each other. At the end, Judge Zhou recognized that the defendant was guilty and sentenced Shen Yuezao to one year and six months in prison. The part of the private suit was ordered to be transferred to the civil court for handling. However, the defendant heard the verdict and refused to accept it. His lawyer declared an appeal, requesting that the defendant be allowed to pay the original guarantee for bail during the appeal period. Therefore, this case, which has been delayed for three years, still needs time to end.

Ma Songting Described the Whole Story of Strangling His Paramour 153

First Saw Another Man in the Room

Suddenly Fled Through the Roof

Killed Because of Jealousy and Hatred

Ma Songting, a native of Suqian, strangled his paramour, Song Qiaobao, a native of Suzhou, in a house at No. 373 Hejian Road on the morning of February 13th of last year. He then stole her jewelry and cash and fled to Nanjing. He was recently arrested by the Capital Police Department and sent to Shanghai by the Patrol Room to be investigated and detained by the Special District Local Court, etc., which has been recorded in this newspaper. It is learned that Ma Songting was united with Song Qiaobao in Wumen. Qiaobao had already been married by her mother, Song Gao, and had two children. Later, after her husband died of illness, she originally wanted to remain a widow, raise her orphans, and learn machine work to make a living. However, since meeting Tingsong, the ancient well was rippled again. Seeing Tingsong in a Western suit, she thought he was a wealthy man at sea, but she did not know that he was only superficial. Hearing that wages in Shanghai were better than in Suzhou, she followed him to Shanghai. Song Gao relied on her daughter for a living, so Qiaobao took her two children and lived with her brother, Ma Tingshou, on Hejian Road. Qiaobao had a lot of private savings, and Songting was addicted to gambling and owed debts, so Qiaobao helped him with money, and their relationship became more affectionate. On the day that Tingsong strangled Qiaobao, according to him, it was because Qiaobao had a lover in the room who was discovered by him. Out of jealousy, he resorted to this means. When the judge asked who the lover was, he said that he had escaped from the roof. However, during the continued trial yesterday, according to Song Gao, her daughter had no other lover, and at that time, she went out to buy noodles, so she did not know the cause of the conflict. But when she left home, her daughter and the defendant were still sitting in the living room, and when she returned, she could not see them. She went upstairs to inspect, but there was no trace. A large leather suitcase was opened, and more than 100 yuan in cash and two gold rings were missing. Her daughter also had 140 yuan and two gold rings and a hollow gold bracelet, all of which were missing. She was still worried that her daughter might have had a quarrel with Songting and went out to commit suicide by jumping into the river, so she went to nearby riverbanks to search and notified her brother, Shoutong, to help search. In the evening, her nephew Erguan wanted to take the package placed under the bed, so she entered the pavilion and saw a foot sticking out. Upon inspection, it was Qiaobao, who had already died. She hurriedly reported to the Patrol Room, who sent detectives to come and carefully inspect the scene under the light. They saw a rope around her neck, which must have been strangled to death, and the defendant has not returned since then. He must have done it, she said. The defendant still confessed that at that time, he came home from outside and was about to go upstairs when he saw a man holding a knife in the pavilion, seeming to want to kill him. Qiaobao frequently shook her head to signal him not to go upstairs. In a moment, the man fled through the roof. He then went upstairs and strangled Qiaobao and immediately ran out, without hiding the body under the bed or stealing gold jewelry and cash. Judge Feng concluded the interrogation and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody pending sentencing.

The Bandit Who Kidnapped Wang Yunwu Was Executed Yesterday 154

The kidnapper, Fei Zhuyu, a native of Shengxian, Shaoxing, was 38 years old. In November of the 15th year of the Republic of China, he colluded with accomplices to kidnap Wang Yunwu, manager of the Commercial Press, on Doule'an Road and Yokohama Road, and hid him in a house at No. 74 Baoyuan Road in Zhabei, demanding a huge ransom. The case was discovered and Fei was apprehended by Shangwu, a Chinese detective of the Huizi Patrol Room. The Special District Court interrogated him and sentenced him to death, and reported it to the Provincial Government for approval and execution. Yesterday afternoon, the due date was reached. Judge Cheng Shangfeng came to the Fifth Criminal Court and ordered Fei Zhuyu to be brought to the case. Judge Cheng announced to Fei that he had received official documents from his superiors today and must execute the death penalty. Did he have any last words? Fei replied that when he was arrested, he had 195 yuan in cash, which was confiscated by the Patrol Room. The money was brought to Shanghai from his hometown to prepare to open a small cigarette paper shop. He was arrested only three days after arriving in Shanghai. Now that he is about to be shot, please take out two yuan to buy food for me, three yuan to buy long ingots, and send the remaining 190 yuan to my brother-in-law Qiu Liansheng at Chongren Town, 30 miles outside the west gate of Shengxian, Shaoxing, to be handed over to my uncle Fei Kaizhi. He has nothing else to say. Then the Patrol Room lawyer said that the cash had been found by the Patrol Room to be the ransom for kidnapping two children in Shaoxing, and Fei had also confessed to it during the trial on December 29th of last year, so it should be confiscated according to law. Judge Cheng then ordered that two yuan be taken out of the court's account box and ordered the officers to buy wine and food for Fei to eat his fill. Then, the detectives, along with the photo files, escorted him to the execution ground in Caohejing in the prisoner's car. He called the Shanghai Local Court to send a prosecutor to the scene and ordered the bailiffs to bring Fei to the case to verify his identity and bind him according to the law for execution by shooting.

Case of Flower Jiqiu's Concubine Filing Charges of Fraudulent Marriage and Abuse 155

Beaten Several Times a Day, Forced to Swallow Opium

Unable to Endure the Suffering, Difficult to Live Together

Demanding Alimony of Five Thousand Yuan

Flower Jiqiu from Jiangxi, currently thirty-six years old and residing at 1625 Jing'an Temple Road, has recently been sued in the Special District Court by his concubine, Flower Zhou, for abandonment and abuse. The indictment states that Flower Jiqiu deceived her into marriage, and after entering his household, she discovered that the defendant already had one wife and one concubine. Since what was done could not be undone, she retreated to the status of a maid. However, she was frequently abused, beaten several times a day, and forced to swallow opium, repeatedly nearing death. She was then driven out and forbidden to live with him, and she is now requesting compensation of five thousand yuan, among other claims. Yesterday, Judge Cheng Shangfeng opened the court to hear the case. Flower Jiqiu testified that he was formerly in the academic world and is now in business. He married the plaintiff as a concubine on July 28th of the eighteenth year [of the Republic], with a contract signed by her birth mother, brother, and matchmaker. They were always harmonious. However, since last year, his birth mother frequently came to stir up trouble, wanting to take his mother back, which he did not allow, leading to disagreements. As for forcing her to swallow gold and opium, it is entirely fabricated. Since she entered the household, he often taught her to read and write, hoping she would improve herself. On November 27th last year, the family was busy entertaining guests, but she was nowhere to be seen. The next day, he found her in her room having taken something with tea. Upon questioning, he learned that she had swallowed [gold] and immediately called a doctor for treatment. After taking medicine for three days without any improvement, he wrote to her mother's house in Suzhou, asking her daughter to come to Shanghai to persuade and advise her. Therefore, he mentioned the matter of swallowing gold in the letter. However, she returned to Suzhou with her mother and never came back. He repeatedly wrote letters urging her, but to no avail. He then went to Suzhou in person, where her family had him arrested by the detective team on false charges of being a bandit. After being proven innocent, he was released. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff still did not let him off and actually used the law to ask him for money to fulfill her other plans, among other things. Flower Zhou stated that she is a Suzhou native, nineteen years old this year, born on September 21st. She married at the age of seventeen, receiving a bride price of five hundred yuan. A birth chart was sent, but she did not know who signed the Flower imprint on the contract. At the time, no wedding ceremony was held. It was said that he had no wife, but after entering the household, she learned that he already had one wife and one concubine. She was usually abused. Now that she has encountered a violent husband, it is difficult to live with him. She has no choice but to return to her mother's house. However, since the plaintiff is still young, she has no means of support for the rest of her life, and since she has already married, it is difficult to marry again. She is requesting a ruling for alimony of thirty yuan per month for fifteen years, totaling five thousand yuan, among other claims. Judge Cheng then instructed the lawyers for the plaintiff and defendant to argue their cases, and a ruling was set for next Thursday. The defendant was ordered to be available for questioning at any time while awaiting the verdict.

Lost Son and Mistress Share a Sweet Dream 156

Unexpectedly, Police Arrive Out of Nowhere

Result: He is Willing to Return Home with His Father

Xu Senbao from Yin County, fifty years old, had a son named Duofang who was enticed by a woman from Changzhou named Weng Gendi, and they planned to marry and live together. Tea Boy Attempts Suicide by Taking Poison 157

Works as a Tea Boy in Sanbei Company

Sent Out to Deliver Four Hundred Yuan, Never Returned

Attempts Suicide in Jue Lu Hotel

Yesterday afternoon around 5 p.m., a man claiming to be Wang Deqing, about thirty years old and in business, arrived at the Jue Lu Hotel on Xizang Road. The tea boy led him to room 95 to rest. In the evening, an old woman, a woman, and a child went to visit him, talked with the guest for a long time, and then left. Yesterday afternoon around 1 p.m., the tea boy routinely asked the guest if he wanted to continue staying, but the door was locked from the inside. After knocking many times without a response, he reported it to the accounting office. The door was broken open, and upon looking inside, everything in the room was as usual. The so-called Wang Deqing was lying stiffly on the bed, barely breathing. Upon inspection, a small can of raw opium was found on the bed, with the paste smeared everywhere, indicating that the guest had taken poison. It was then known that the guest had committed suicide by taking poison. The matter was immediately reported to the Zhabei police station, who dispatched detectives to investigate. Wang Deqing was immediately taken to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he was unable to be saved due to the overdose. Afterwards, a "Shen Shun" receipt book was found in the room, with the words "Sanbei Shipping Company" on it. Upon inquiry by the hotel, it was learned that the person who committed suicide was actually a tea boy from the Sanbei Shipping Company named Yao Shunjin, a native of Ningbo. The name Wang Deqing was an alias. It is said that Yao went out to deliver four hundred yuan one afternoon and never returned that night. Last year, he also attempted suicide with tranquilizer water.

Public Bus Collides with Tram 165

Two Drivers Argue Endlessly

The Tram Service is Interrupted

At 7:35 last night, Public Bus No. 4090 on the Hua Merchants' Second Route, traveling from Longhua to Laoximen, was turning south near the Chen Ying Shi Memorial Tower in Ximen when it accidentally collided with Tram No. 40 on the Hua Merchants' Third Route, traveling from Yuan Route from north to south. American Ship Houston to Arrive in Shanghai 169

The Great American Evening Post said that the flagship of the United States Asiatic Fleet, the Houston, will arrive in Shanghai around the 15th of this month. The ship was originally scheduled to come directly to Shanghai from Xiamen, but the plan has been changed to arrive at Songkou on April 5th to load mail and then sail up the river to Beijing. It is expected to arrive there on the morning of the 7th. Fleet Commander Rear Admiral Mikeville will visit government officials in Beijing. If he can complete his official business in time, he plans to set sail for Shanghai on the morning of the 15th. Because the American naval buoy in the Huangpu River cannot moor a ship as large as the Houston (600 feet long and 66 feet wide, the current naval treaty stipulates that warships are limited to this size, so the ship can be called the largest in the navy), it will be anchored near the 10th and 23rd buoys of the Ruirong Shipyard. The American naval authorities have asked the Customs to expand the warship berthing area in the Huangpu River, but have not been granted permission, because the Customs is currently trying to order all warships to leave the buoys in the Huangpu River to avoid hindering commercial navigation.

Difficulties After the Reform of the Songhu Railway 170

Frequent Delays

Crowded Passengers

After the Songhu Railway switched to steam engines, the number of daily round trips increased to seventy-four. Since the 15th of last month, the number of daily trips has been changed to forty, but the number of trips between Jiangwan and Shanghai has been increased to eighty-two. The steam locomotives that have been freed up are used as reserves to avoid delays caused by damaged vehicles. The Railway Bureau also declared that if there are crowded passengers on the entire line, the Railway Bureau can still specially open locomotives and attach vehicles to accommodate the passengers. However, it has been more than half a month since the implementation of the reform. The Shanghai-Jiangwan section is indeed convenient, but the passengers on each round trip between Songhu are extremely crowded. In the afternoon, many passengers who have purchased tickets are unable to board the train. The Railway Bureau should take measures to rectify this.

Coal Industry Association Temporary Meeting 171

Discussing the Kailuan's Failure to Deliver Coal as Agreed

The Coal Industry Association is discussing a solution because the Kailuan Sales Office has failed to deliver coal as agreed, causing a dispute. Therefore, a discussion meeting was held at 2:30 yesterday, chaired by Mao Chunpu. Lu Qisheng, Pan Yisan, Yan Yangshan, and others expressed their opinions, all of whom believed that the claim by the Kailuan Sales Office that transportation on the Beining Road was difficult was inconsistent with the evidence obtained by the association from various sources. It was confirmed that the Sales Office had other intentions and deliberately breached its contract, resulting in industrial manufacturers feeling the fear of coal shortages and causing social disputes. The association previously sent a letter to the Sales Office for inquiries, but the Sales Office did not respond with the facts. Therefore, the Sales Office should be responsible for everything. Zhang Zhangkui of Yuantai Company said that the Sales Office has not been able to announce the truth about the difficult transportation on the Beining Road, so their four companies have not received any news and cannot answer the questions of their fellow traders. Luo Deyou, Bao Zhexiong, and others said that recently, fellow traders have been forced to buy other types of expensive coal to compensate their customers due to the Kailuan coal shortage, incurring a subsidy of about 23.4 taels per ton. This is a last resort for fellow traders to maintain their reputation with customers. After several discussions, it was decided to convene a mediation meeting between the two parties on April 9th in accordance with the association's constitution, in order to quickly and peacefully resolve the dispute and avoid further conflicts.
